v1.32.0) does NOT use sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime internally. Instead, it implements its own controller-manager framework via the staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager module.\\n\\n## Reconciler / Controller Interface\\n\\nThe base interface for all controllers is `controller.Interface` defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go`. It requires only a `Name() string` method. Controllers may also optionally implement `Debuggable` (to expose debug HTTP handlers) and `HealthCheckable` (to report health status). The actual reconcile loop is not mandated by an interface—each controller implements its own `Run(ctx, workers)` method internally.\\n\\nA more generic reconciler pattern (with a `reconciler func(namespace, name string, newObj T) error` callback) exists in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/internal/generic/controller.go` for the admission policy subsystem.\\n\\n## SetupWithManager Equivalent: InitFunc and ControllerDescriptor\\n\\nIn place of controller-runtime's `SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager)`, Kubernetes uses the `InitFunc` type defined in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`:\\n\\n```go\\ntype InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\\n```\\n\\nEach controller is wrapped in a `ControllerDescriptor` struct that pairs the name with its `InitFunc`. The init function creates the controller, wires it to informers from `ControllerContext.InformerFactory`, and launches the controller's reconcile loop via `go controller.Run(ctx, workers)`.\\n\\nExample (in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/apps.go`):\\n```go\\nfunc newDaemonSetControllerDescriptor() *ControllerDescriptor {\\n    return &ControllerDescriptor{\\n        name:     names.DaemonSetController,\\n        initFunc: startDaemonSetController,\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## Wiring into the Manager Reconcile Loop\\n\\n1. `NewControllerDescriptors()` in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go` — registers all known controllers by calling each `newXxxControllerDescriptor()` factory.\\n2. `CreateControllerContext()` — creates the `ControllerContext` (shared informer factories, REST mapper, client builder).\\n3. `StartControllers()` — iterates over all enabled `ControllerDescriptor`s and calls `StartController()` for each.\\n4. `StartController()` — invokes `controllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()(ctx, controllerCtx, name)`, which wires the controller to informers and starts its reconcile goroutine.\\n5. After all controllers are started, `controllerContext.InformerFactory.Start(stopCh)` begins the shared informers.\\n\\nThe per-controller reconcile loop (`Run` method) processes events from a `workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface`, calling an internal `syncHandler` (e.g., `syncDeployment`, `syncDaemonSet`) that performs the actual reconciliation of desired vs. actual state—the functional equivalent of controller-runtime's `Reconcile(ctx, req)` method.\\n\\nThe entry point is `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:Run()` which calls `StartControllers()` and starts the informers, completing the wiring of all controllers into the manager's reconcile loop.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2527,"cache_read_input_tokens":80555,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":2527,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"420d7f54-e760-43ef-9f25-1dba771ecc86","uuid":"775e811a-97c8-4154-8228-21ed7b632693"}

Instead, it implements its own controller-manager framework via the staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager module.\\n\\n## Reconciler / Controller Interface\\n\\nThe base interface for all controllers is `controller.Interface` defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go`. After controllers start, `controllerContext.InformerFactory.Start(stopCh)` and `controllerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory.Start(stopCh)` begin the shared informers.\\n\\nThe per-controller reconcile loop (`Run` method) processes events from a `workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface`, calling an internal sync handler that performs reconciliation — the functional equivalent of controller-runtime's `Reconcile(ctx, req)` method.\\n\\nThe top-level entry point is `Run()` in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`, which calls `CreateControllerContext` and `StartControllers`, completing the wiring of all controllers into the manager's reconcile loop.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":355,"cache_read_input_tokens":86881,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":355,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"420d7f54-e760-43ef-9f25-1dba771ecc86","uuid":"2e653d72-2696-4b8c-bcc4-e27817c36fdb"}
